				<div class="row">
					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">

						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

			<!--=== Content ===-->
			<div class="container content height-500">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">
								<div class="panel panel-grey margin-bottom-40">
									<div class="panel-heading">
										<h3 class="panel-title">CIDR to IP Range</h3>
									</div>
									<div class="panel-body">
										<form method="post">
											<div>
			<h3>Result</h3>
			<div style="overflow-x:auto;">
			<table class="table table-striped">
				<tobdy>
					<tr>
						<th>CIDR Range</th>
						<td>10.10.0.0/16</td>
					</tr>
					<tr>
						<th>Netmask</th>
						<td>255.255.0.0</td>
					</tr>
					<tr>
						<th>Wildcard Bits</th>
						<td>0.0.255.255</td>
					</tr>
					<tr>
						<th>First IP</th>
						<td><a href="https://www.ip2location.com/demo/10.10.0.0" target="_blank">10.10.0.0</a></td>
					</tr>
					<tr>
						<th>First IP (Decimal)</th>
						<td>168427520</td>
					</tr>
					<tr>
						<th>Last IP</th>

			<div class="container content height-500">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">

							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">
								<div class="panel panel-grey margin-bottom-40">
									<div class="panel-heading">
										<h3 class="panel-title">CIDR to IP Range</h3>
									</div>
									<div class="panel-body">
										<form method="post">
											<div>

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">

			<div class="container content height-500">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">

			<div class="container content height-500">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">

						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">

					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">

			<div class="container content height-500">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">

			<div class="container content height-500">
				<div class="row">
					<div class="col-md-9">
						<div class="margin-bottom-40">
							<p>
								CIDR is the short for Classless Inter-Domain Routing, an IP addressing scheme that replaces the older system based on classes A, B, and C. 
								A single IP address can be used to designate many unique IP addresses with CIDR. A CIDR IP address looks like a normal IP address except that it ends with a slash followed by a number, called the IP network prefix. 
								CIDR addresses reduce the size of routing tables and make more IP addresses available within organizations. Please try out our CIDR calculator below.
							</p>
						</div>

						<div class="row margin-bottom-40">
							<div class="col-md-12">
